Record of the Citizens' Assembly Delegate Meeting 177

The Citizens' Federation convened a delegate meeting of various district branches at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. More than 90 delegates from the branches were present, and Hu Fengxiang was publicly elected as chairman. After the formalities were completed, the following matters were discussed: (A) As party and national leaders are all gathered in Shanghai, how should the federation express its opinion? Zhang Zilian, Wang Zhaocheng, Liu Zhongying, Yan Esheng, Wang Yansong, Yu Zhongxian, Cao Zhigong, Cheng Xiechun, Wang Baihe and others expressed their opinions and resolved that the federation should issue a statement on the current situation: (1) Urge party and national leaders to quickly consult on major party and national plans and decide on a diplomatic policy towards Japan. (2) (Omitted) (B) How should the federation express its opinion on foreign affairs? It was resolved to send a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which was then forwarded to Minister Shi in Geneva, stating that the principle of no direct negotiations between China and Japan must be upheld and that efforts must be made to ensure that Japan unconditionally withdraws its troops and reserves compensation for various damages and losses in the three northeastern provinces. As for how to punish Japan after the withdrawal of troops, it was requested that the League of Nations make a fair judgment to maintain world peace. (C) How should the federation prevent Japanese ruffians from repeatedly smashing the glass windows of stores on North Sichuan Road, etc.? It was resolved to send a letter to the Public Works Department, holding them responsible for insufficient protection, and demanding that the Public Works Department compensate for the losses of smashed glass windows, and to send a letter to the Public Security Bureau to dispatch capable police officers to protect the border. (D) Wang Zhaocheng, Liu Zhongying and Xu Yunhui proposed that the federation's Japanese Goods Inspection Committee was facing difficulties due to the publication of advertisements by the Anti-Japanese Association. How should this be resolved? Wang Jian'e, Lin Yangzhi, Zhang Chiseng, Qiu Liangyu, Chen Jiufeng, Ye Jiaxing and others expressed their opinions and resolved that (1) a letter should be sent to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to correct the previous advertisements to avoid misunderstandings among stores; (2) each branch should organize an inspection team, which must be submitted to the federation for forwarding to the Anti-Japanese Association; (3) goods sealed by trade associations and registered with the federation need not be sealed again, and those not sealed should be sealed by the federation. The meeting adjourned at 1:00 p.m.

Two Organizations Jointly Certify Domestic Goods 179

Baoxing Factory Asks for Instructions

Shanghai Baoxing Mineral Powder Factory sent a letter to the Joint Association of Machine-Made Domestic Goods Factories, stating: "We respectfully inform you that since the Wanbaoshan incident, public outrage has been aroused, and domestic organizations are being formed to achieve the goal of economic severance. Your association, with its enthusiasm and insight, has taken the lead in organizing a domestic goods certification group, publishing advertisements for certification to provide identification. In promoting domestic goods and resisting enemy goods, it has been well received. Our factory admires this and has applied for certification of our completely domestic gemstone trademark pencils, etc. In recent days, the violent Japanese have forcibly occupied the Northeast, and their aggression is even more serious. Various organizations are conducting inspections and sealing off goods with extraordinary rigor in order to thoroughly resist them. This shows that the hearts of the people are not dead. However, reading the newspaper reports on October 17th, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice on domestic goods certification, with attached application rules, and on October 20th, the seventh clause of the resolution of the Committee for Economic Severance Against Japan, stating that goods with the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's domestic goods certificate should be released. Although the organizations are different, the purpose is to facilitate all sectors, recognize domestic goods, and avoid misunderstandings, which is the same as your association's purpose. However, our factory has some doubts. If a domestic good has already been certified by your association, but the procedures are not yet complete at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, can it be exempt from difficulties in sales across the country? If a misunderstanding occurs, does your association have any corresponding guarantees? This matter is of great importance to the future of domestic goods and your association's reputation. Should you contact the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Anti-Japanese Association in advance to avoid unexpected twists and turns for domestic goods factories? We believe that high-minded people must have considered this and have a satisfactory solution. Our factory, attached to the end, dares not remain silent. What is the actual situation? We hope you will announce your instructions, and we are looking forward to it."

Reader's Correspondence

How to Effectively Boycott Japanese Goods, Lin Yifang 193

(1) Everyone should start with themselves, carefully examining whether the things they need for clothing, food, housing, and transportation are Japanese goods. Everyone should adhere to the principle of using domestic goods. (2) Managers of businesses nationwide should pay special attention when procuring goods, ensuring that they are indeed domestic goods before purchasing them. This can prevent ordinary people without knowledge from mistakenly buying Japanese goods. (3) Customs inspectors should conduct thorough investigations to prevent smuggling by unscrupulous merchants. The highest tax rates should be imposed on imported Japanese goods, so that they will voluntarily cease importing them even before the boycott is fully implemented. (This clause, which prohibits arbitrary increases or decreases in tax rates for goods from various countries, is not feasible. - Editor's Note) (4) The government should order police officers in all areas to pay special attention to searching for Japanese goods as a long-term responsibility. (Boycotting Japanese goods is a matter for the people, and cannot be handled by the government. This clause is not feasible. - Editor's Note) (5) When seeing friends buying or selling Japanese goods, they should be kindly advised to understand Japan's ambitions and voluntarily refrain from buying and selling them. (6) Merchants nationwide must not take advantage of the boycott of Japanese goods as an opportunity to profit, or even pass off inferior goods as domestic goods and raise prices to deceive people. If such behavior occurs, the most severe methods should be used for punishment. The above are a few of my temporary thoughts. I hope that all compatriots nationwide can have self-respect and seriously implement the boycott, so that the ultimate goal can be achieved amidst the boycott.

Weather Report 195

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Cloudy and cold in the Yangtze River basin; strong northwesterly winds along the Shandong coast; gentle cyclones in the East China Sea due to the passage of a small low-pressure system moving towards the northeast-east; severe weather between the Ogasawara and Ryukyu Islands due to a hurricane moving towards the northeast-north. The hurricane center was within 120 miles of the intersection of 25 degrees north latitude and 136 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM this afternoon. Furthermore, in the 24 hours prior to 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 75.7 degrees Fahrenheit, and the lowest was 49.9 degrees Fahrenheit. On the same day last year, the highest was 72.3 degrees Fahrenheit, and the lowest was 59.9 degrees Fahrenheit.

Removing the Weeds in the Courtyard - Random Musings by Zhaifu

The Death of Edison (Part 1) 196

The American inventor Thomas Edison died at home this month on the 18th at the old age of 84. To live is a great matter; to die is also a great matter. To die as he did can be considered a death without regret.

From 1869, when his first invention was announced, to 1910, his inventions, large and small, totaled 1,328. During this period, he averaged one invention every eleven days. After 1910, with more assistants, his inventive career became even smoother, leaving others far behind.

Among these inventions, the most influential are undoubtedly the electric light, the streetcar, the motion picture camera, the phonograph, and the sound film. Although the telephone was invented by Bell, it could not have been widely used without Edison's invention of the carbon microphone. Even in scientifically backward China, few people in the cities are not affected by Edison's influence. When we turn on the electric light, ride the streetcar, watch a movie, or listen to the phonograph, we should remember this old man's contribution to humanity.

Anecdotes About Edison, the King of Invention 197

— Yi Weisheng

Edison, the eccentric genius of the electrical world, started out as a newsboy. He neither received higher education nor studied under famous teachers. However, with his extraordinary understanding and tireless learning, he achieved great success and became one of the most prominent figures in the world. Americans even revered him as the King of Invention. He passed away at his home at 3:24 AM on October 18th of this year, and the world was shocked and mourned. Throughout his life, he emphasized experimentation in his studies. This can be seen from the fact that he began setting up a laboratory in the basement of his home at the age of twelve. Although he also enjoyed reading, his readings were mostly in the natural sciences. He lived to the age of eighty-four. In the spring of the year before his death, he still prayed to heaven, wishing to live another five years to complete his unfinished work, as he was experimenting with extracting rubber from the essence of sage. Edison had many unusual characteristics throughout his life, some of which are worth recording as follows:

He dropped out of school very early, and his grades in school were always below average. He liked to smoke and chew tobacco.

He never paid attention to the grooming of his appearance.

He was repeatedly dismissed from various jobs.

He never paid attention to his private property.

He often conducted chemical experiments that endangered the lives of many people.

He strongly opposed the idea of sleeping eight hours a day.

He liked to smoke strong black cigars and strictly forbade his subordinates from smoking paper cigarettes.

His knowledge of common commercial affairs was extremely shallow. At the age of twenty-eight, he still did not know how to cash a check. When someone told him how to cash it, he cashed the check for 40,000 gold dollars for the invention rights of the stock ticker, taking ten-dollar and five-dollar bills, and guarded it all night, not knowing that he should deposit this large sum in the bank.

He did not care about registering to protect his invention rights, so the amount of losses in this area was enormous.

He did not like to buy new clothes. He always wore clothes that were tattered and worn, but he did not easily change them.

When going out in the evening, he always wore silk clothes and liked to use a square-foot-sized Indian silk handkerchief.

When reading a newspaper, he could read three lines at a glance, and he already understood the news in his heart.

He liked humor and always made himself the object of his humorous writing. For example, "When I was in diapers, I lived on milk and didn't like it. Now I'm back to my milk life. It's ridiculous." "I have been engaged in two kinds of work throughout my life. Most people also engage in two kinds of work, and one of them is playing cards."

He believed that the greatest benefit of his invention of the incandescent light bulb was that it could help people sleep less. He believed that excessive food and excessive sleep were the two major bad habits of mankind.

Edison's daily sleep of only four hours had become a common topic of conversation. However, his friend Fiston admitted that Edison did not often doze off during the day.

In Memory of Qiu Xue'an Public Sacrifice to Lyricists 199

— Sun Choucheng

Attached to the Qiu Xue'an Temple in Hangzhou is a shrine to lyricists from the two Zhe provinces throughout the ages. Every late autumn, the reed flowers bloom in full bloom, pure white like snow. The autumn wind rustles, and the reed flowers sway with the wind, resembling white waves. The literati of the two Zhe provinces hold a public sacrifice on a selected date after the Frost's Descent solar term, and feast and drink while appreciating the reeds. When the public sacrifice was held in the eighteenth year, Choucheng happened to be in Wulin and participated. Recently, I received a letter from a friend in Hangzhou, saying that the reeds were already flying like snow, inviting me to appreciate them together. Due to numerous matters, I was unable to find time to leave. Therefore, I recorded the sights and sounds from when I participated in the public sacrifice to the lyricists the year before, to record my spiritual journey.

Travelers from other provinces to Hangzhou only know to visit West Lake, and do not know to visit Xixi. This is because West Lake is located on the sunny side of the mountains of Qiantangmen West and Fahua Qinting, and is known to all because it has been praised by people in poems. Xixi is located on the shady side of the mountains, stretching for more than thirty miles, no more than a foot wide in narrow places, and no more than a few fathoms wide in wide places. Sandy islands are winding, and one cannot see the end at a glance. The area is planted with reeds, rushes, and reeds. In late autumn, one can row a small boat with close friends and travel along the stream. Everything is white and glistening, pressing low against the back of the awning. This scene is far better than West Lake. There is a Qiu Xue'an Temple here, originally named Dasheng. The Xianchun Lin'an Zhi states that there is a Dasheng sentence in the depths of the rushes, referring to this temple. In the early years of Chunxi in the Song Dynasty, it was the Jingbie courtyard of Zen Master Zishou. It was named after the monk's name. Later, Chen Meigong extracted the meaning of the Tang poem "Autumn Snow Covers a Fishing Boat" and changed the name to the current name. It had long been destroyed. In the year of Wuwu, Wu Cheng Zhou Qingyun traveled here and was moved, and raised money to rebuild it. He also attached a shrine to the lyricists of the two Zhe provinces throughout the ages. In the autumn of Renxu, Kang Nanhai traveled here and joined Xia Dinghou and others in writing linked verses after drinking. They were immediately carved on a stone tablet and embedded in the wall. The text reads: "The reed flowers rustle, filling the continent. The flowers fly to swallow the Yunmeng Lake. One gains a clear tour outside the mountains and lakes. Autumn ages the Xixi sky and water colors. There is a boat trip with Nanhai's seat. I have the honor of accompanying the staff and shoes to appreciate the autumn snow." The plaque with the four characters "Spirit of the Thatched Cottage" hangs high in the shrine. The spirit tablets of the lyricists of the two Zhe provinces throughout the ages are enshrined in the middle. The spirit tablets of the four types of lyricists - officials traveling, exiles, outsiders, and women in boudoirs - are attached on the sides. The couplets hanging on the walls were written by Zhu Xiaozang. The text reads: "Coming and going day and night, this place should have lyricist immortals, embracing plain clouds and yellow cranes." "The reed flowers share the same color, and the lonely guest sings sad verses again, facing thousands of ravines and cliffs." There is a Finger-Snapping Tower in the temple. From the tower, one can see the distant mountains with their deep and beautiful forests standing facing each other. Looking down, one sees the

A Chronology of Japanese Aggression Against China and Various Massacres (Part 1) 200

— Moyi

It has been more than a month since Japan forcibly occupied the Eastern Provinces. Our country is still embracing non-resistance and maintaining a calm policy, waiting for the League of Nations to resolve the situation. However, the League of Nations has held two meetings, and its trend seems to have succumbed to Japanese violence. The effectiveness of the League of Nations that our country imagined is actually equal to zero. Currently, both the Ning and Yue factions will hold a peace conference in Shanghai, hoping that there will be some improvement in the foreign policy to live up to the expectations of the people and suppress the fierce flames of Japan. The following is a chronology of Japanese aggression against China and various massacres, as a final reckoning with the tyrant.

In the 20th year of the Wanli reign (1592), Japan dispatched 130,000 soldiers and 9,000 sailors to attack the vassal state of Korea. This was the beginning of Japanese imperialism's aggression against China.

In the 21st year of the Wanli reign (1593), Korea suffered from the Japanese army and begged for aid from the Ming Dynasty. The Ming court responded to the request of the Korean king and sent troops to rescue them, but they were defeated by the Japanese army.

In the 37th year of the Wanli reign (1609), the Japanese general Tokugawa Hidetada ordered Shimazu Iehisa to invade our Ryukyu, capturing King Sho Nei and subjugating Ryukyu to the Satsuma domain, supervising its finances, and stipulating that the crown prince must visit Te'er Island every year at the age of fifteen.

During March of the 10th year of the Tongzhi reign (1874), the Japanese government appointed Lieutenant General Saigo Tsugumichi of the army as the governor of Taiwan affairs, leading the navy to forcibly occupy Taiwan, and beheading the chief Alu and his sons, among others.

During February of the 2nd year of the Guangxu reign (1876), Japan signed a commercial treaty with our vassal state of Korea, forcing Korea to secede from China as an autonomous country.

In the 5th year of the Guangxu reign (1879), the Japanese government sent Minister of the Imperial Household Ito Hirobumi and Minister of Agriculture Saigo Tsugumichi to our country to discuss the Korean treaty. Our Qing court sent Li Hongzhang as the national minister, and Wu Dazheng as his deputy. They opened discussions in Tianjin. At that time, Li Hongzhang and others did not understand diplomacy and signed a treaty with Japan with three clauses, actually recognizing Korea as a country under joint Chinese and Japanese protection.

In the 21st year of the Guangxu reign (1895), the Donghak Party incident broke out in Korea. Japan immediately sent troops to Korea. On June 20th, the Japanese envoy Otori Keisuke led troops into the Korean palace, killing the guards and capturing King Li Hee, using the Daewongun to preside over state affairs, and exiling Min Young-joon and others to Evil Island. All Korean officials who were not pro-Japanese were killed. Our country sent troops to rescue them, but they were defeated by the Japanese army. Thereupon, Japan used force to coerce us into signing the Treaty of Shimonoseki with eleven clauses, forcing us to recognize Korea as an autonomous country, ceding Taiwan, the Penghu Islands, and other places, opening Shashi, Chongqing, Suzhou, and Hangzhou as trading ports, and demanding reparations of 200 million taels of silver.

Below the tower is a bridge called Wohong, which leads to the reed marsh. Each person has a biography published in a special book for exhibition. During the sacrifice, sacrificial offerings are displayed on the altar, and ancient music is played on both sides. A Sick Man in the Midst of National Crisis 201

— Su Min, Sent from Hankou

China has always been known to the world as a sick man. Therefore, there are many sick men in the country. It is painful to say. This time, the Japanese invaders treat our people like nothing. Anyone with a little blood and spirit is filled with grief and indignation, vowing to fight the Japanese to the death. I once attended military school as a young man and have a slight understanding of military knowledge. However, due to a lack of promotion, I turned to the academic world and lived a cold and lonely life. In the quiet of the night, I often lament the growth of the flesh on my thighs. Seeing the national crisis at hand, I originally wanted to put down my pen and join the army to exert my strength for the country. However, due to excessive depression in recent years, I contracted hemoptysis. Despite taking medicine, it had no effect. My lung qi is declining daily, and my body is weak and powerless. Although I want to follow in the footsteps of Ban Chao, what can I do when the disease is trapping me and my strength is not enough? The other day, I wrote to my friend Wang Zizhong in Shanghai, discussing the state of the country and mentioning my illness, regretting that I could not join the volunteer army. Wang Zi and I have always been close friends. He immediately sent me a package of magic medicine, saying it was Yijin Cao produced by Peisheng Pharmaceutical Company, which can radically cure pulmonary tuberculosis and hemoptysis. I can give it a try. If I can recover from my chronic illness one day, I can still take up arms and go to the front to serve my country. I was overjoyed to receive the medicine and immediately tried it. The cough stopped indeed. After ten days, my physical strength gradually recovered. I realized that if I could not turn weakness into strength, this body would still be useful. If something happened to the country one day, I would definitely join the army and fulfill my lifelong ambition. I would destroy this enemy with every meal. The day is approaching. I was so happy that I couldn't sleep for a while, so I took up my pen to write this down.

The Novel Club

The Pestle of Dreams (23) 202

— Cheng Zhanlu

"Isn't that the certain army commander who implemented the breaking of cauldrons and sinking of boats?" He pointed at a young military officer dancing in the Palace of Confusion, muttering to himself.

"This army commander, because of foreign insults pressing the border and the shame of the nation, once implemented the method of breaking cauldrons and sinking boats, bravely fighting the enemy and driving them out of the country, is someone everyone admires; why is he also dancing here?"

The young military officer kissed the dancing girl passionately several times, and, hand in hand, in unison, sang the "Tatta Song":

丨丨Tatta Song, Tatta Song; if I don't enjoy myself now, what am I waiting for?

Singing and dancing under the Kaoshan Hall, as stable as Mount Tai 丨 as firm as a rock 丨

丨丨Tatta Song, Tatta Song: if I don't enjoy myself now, what am I waiting for?

Kaoshan Hall is the Palace of Peace and Happiness, entertaining with clear songs 丨 embellished with wonderful dances 丨

丨丨Tatta Song, Tatta Song: if I don't enjoy myself now, what am I waiting for?

Under Kaoshan Hall, no one insults, so let's be happy 丨 let's sing and dance 丨

Just as he was singing the third stanza of the "Tatta Song," suddenly a gust of black wind from beyond the heavens blew in, causing pearly tears and jade laments in the dance floor, and scattering the shadows of people 丨 blowing this Kaoshan Hall, as stable as Mount Tai and as firm as a rock, shaking it a few times, almost causing it to collapse completely 丨 Tao Chi, stimulated by this unexpected shock, suddenly, in his dark mind, there came a beam of light like a searchlight 丨 In this light, he saw again the scene of himself entering the Wu'ai Nunnery and talking with the elder, and could not help but feel warned by his conscience, and lament to himself 丨

"Alas 丨 This is bad 丨 I have actually sunk into the vortex of modernity 丨 If I want to escape the vortex, I must strive to pull myself out: if I want to strive to pull myself out, I must shout loudly for the elder of the Wu'ai Nunnery 丨"

He had already made up his mind 丨 He was going to call out for the elder of the Wu'ai Nunnery 丨 But, as if in a nightmare, his heart wanted to shout for the elder of the Wu'ai Nunnery, but his mouth would not obey 丨

He became even more panicked 丨 If he could not shout the five characters "elder of the Wu'ai Nunnery," he would only sink forever into the vortex of modernity 丨

"Wu'ai..." He could only shout two characters.

"What Wu'ai, Wu'ai, this is the real Wu'ai (unobstructed)!" A dancing girl, holding Tao Chi's neck, said very intimately.

Gold Price Rises Six Taels 203

The upward trend. Yesterday, the standard gold price suddenly rose again, showing a firm and advantageous state. However, there were more than eight taels of retrospective price adjustments in the morning and afternoon. People's sentiment turned higher, and in the end, the price was raised by six taels. The fluctuations were still stable. It seemed that the silver market's rise did not affect it. The initial opening was slightly higher, already becoming an inverse proportion. Indeed, the American silver market rose slightly, especially because there were telegraphic communications from the UK stating they would maintain gold coins. Moreover, the bills of exchange from the UK and the US turned from a deficit to a surplus. Although it was a long release, internally it was tense. The buying sentiment in the market was consistently high, and soon after it broke through 705 taels or more. However, Hengxing and others sold quite a bit, resulting in slight advances and retreats. Finally, it was at 706 or 7 taels. The market will be closed tomorrow, as it is Saturday. Recalling this week, the market situation has changed significantly. In reality, both the domestic and international situations are complex, and people's hearts are hesitant. The price was as low as 685 taels and as high as 722 taels. The total increase was about 13 taels. The winds and waves of the future will be difficult to calm down. However, the gold exchange's margin has been reduced by ten taels, and it is now thirty taels (per bar). It was already announced to all brokers yesterday.

Fluctuations are still stable. From the early opening, it increased by 1 tael and 5 mace to 701 taels. Large bars rebounded from 8/6 to 16/9. The silver price only increased by 1/2. Private telegrams only increased by 1/4. Therefore, it continued to rise by 1 tael and a half, to 02 taels and a half. Hengxing came to sell, and it was reduced by 3 taels, to 699 taels and 5 mace. Before long, the face was still good. Qian Changxiang, Zhifeng, Yonghengchangyong and others bought, and the bills of exchange tended to be firm. The bank traded US dollars at 32 yuan 3125, and when the opening bell rang, it was 04 taels and 5 mace, while Changsan (Shanghai) was listed at 375. Then HSBC sold forward US dollars at 32 yuan. Afterwards, short-term zero accounts covered their positions, and Mitsui absorbed US dollars at 32 yuan, so it increased by 2 taels. American Cotton Harvest is Likely to be Delayed 214

Due to Humid Weather

Speculative Spot Hoarding

New York, Telegram of the 23rd, reporting on the cotton market during the week: At the beginning of last week, the price of cotton continued to strengthen due to the continued movement of the buying wind. Although there was a reaction afterwards, when the price fell, the industry and speculators bought in, so the situation was quite stable, and the selling in the South was also slight. The humid climate has delayed the harvest in the fields, but in the mid-month report of the ginning number, it is expected to break various records. According to private estimates, the ginning number ending on October 18 may reach 8 million to 9 million bales. It is also heard that many news say that speculators are widely buying spot goods in the Southern market in preparation for hoarding.

Yesterday's futures wheat market saw prices rise throughout the morning and afternoon. Over 200 Bundles of Jiangbei Waste Silk Transported to Shanghai 220

Jiangbei counties have all reported droughts this year. All silk cocoon waste products are being transported by cargo owners to Nanjing for storage. Due to the receding waters, there is still cargo from Jiangbei production areas that has not been shipped out, and it is now being transported in batches. As a result, Nanjing warehouses are running out of space. Therefore, Li He and other firms are transporting the Jiangbei residue, cocoon ends, handles, cocoon head, and cocoon skin that was previously stored in various Nanjing warehouses to Shanghai by truck. Yesterday, 250 items arrived and are currently stored in the railway bureau's warehouse for collection. More than 300 bundles are expected to continue to arrive in Shanghai in the coming days.

Social News Marshal Foch

Diary of the European War (Translated by Gu Angruo) 224

Allocation of American Troops as of October 20:

(1) On the French front of the Allied forces (French and British): 3 divisions in the Vosges region, 2 divisions in the French 4th Army region, 2 divisions in the Franchet d'Espèrey Army region, and 1 division scattered in various units.

2 divisions on the British front.

(2) Under the command of General Pershing:

14 divisions on the front lines in the Argonne and Lorraine regions, 6 divisions on the second lines, 9 divisions in the rear, and 4 newly arrived divisions.

A total of 43 divisions.

According to the table above, of the 30 divisions fighting on the front lines, 10 divisions are allocated to the Allied forces (French and British), and 20 divisions are under the command of General Pershing. These 20 divisions form the independent American forces.

The American forces are divided into two parts, each with a different nature. For various reasons, this allocation was made. I also plan to implement a strategy of shifting resources as the situation evolves, reducing the 20-division portion to increase the 10-division portion. In this way, the weaknesses of the American commander-in-chief can be reduced. However, no one can deny the courageous fighting of the American troops. After capturing Saint-Mihiel on September 12, the American troops attacked Argonne on September 26. From September 26 to October 20, the American troops suffered 54,158 casualties. The main reason is that the terrain in the battle area is narrow, making it difficult for large forces to maneuver, and attacking against a strong enemy is not worth the losses.

At the same time, in order to promote the rapid restoration of the joint offensive of the French 4th Army and the American 1st Army and to facilitate their attack, I issued a general instruction on October 21, clearly stipulating the objectives and strategies to be used by each army as follows:

The general objective of the American 1st Army and the right wing of the French 4th Army is for the American 1st Army to advance to the Buzancy area and for the French 4th Army to advance to Le Chesne, in order to break through the Aisne River line from the east.

The two armies have achieved complete contact through fighting so far. The American army was previously blocked by the forest area, but now it can take the opportunity to attack. The two armies should identify a common goal and first occupy the high ground of Argonne with a large-scale operation from the east and west. In this way, the unnecessary sacrifices in the forest war can be avoided. The successful steps are as follows:

(1) The American 1st Army should prepare to launch a powerful attack towards Buzancy as soon as possible, using the open area north of Romagne and Romont, and avoiding engagement in the forests of Argonne and Bantheville. Only in this way can the objective be achieved.

(2) The French 4th Army should maintain contact with the American army at Grandpré, while using a large-scale, rapid maneuver to attack Champigneulle from Vuzier, and Le Châtelet from Vouziers, directly taking Le Chesne and striving to expand the front line. The commanders of the American army and the Central Army Group must be informed of the above instructions so that the two armies can expand the scope of operations according to the plan and meet at the designated objective. Please inform me of how the two army commanders are coordinating. My plan is for the French and American armies to conduct expanded attacks in the easy-to-maneuver areas on both sides of Argonne.

I then urged General Pershing to begin the offensive west of the Meuse River as soon as possible. On October 27, I wrote to him, "It is most important for the American 1st Army to prepare to launch an offensive on the scheduled date, that is, November 1, and it must continue to advance until the great victory is achieved."

I also stipulated that after the American 1st Army launched its offensive on November 1, it must continue to advance until it occupied Buzancy before halting.

The development of the French 4th Army east of Vouziers since October 13 facilitated the American operations. The French army established bridgeheads between Vandy and Falaise on the right bank of the Aisne River, containing large German forces in the Argonne region, thereby greatly reducing the pressure on the American army.

The American army began its offensive on November 1, and on the first day, it captured enemy positions in the Buzancy-Stonne area. On the left flank, the French 4th Army also expanded to the east of the Aisne River. I then ordered the French and American armies to take advantage of the victory and advance towards Sedan and Mézières. (To be continued)

Social News Manuscript Guidelines 225

(1) The text should be related to domestic and foreign news about science, industry, commerce, agriculture, (2) sanitation, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life. Pictures should be limited to lyrical paintings about various social life.

(3) Photographs of seasonal events, landscapes, diligence, people, and news-related photography are qualified. Photographs of seasonal landscapes with beauties are especially welcome.

Book and Newspaper Reviews

Yu Yang: Japan's Tanaka Cabinet's Aggressive Policy of Invading Manchuria and Mongolia 226

The Shanghai Xin Sheng News Agency Publishing Department has translated Japan's Tanaka Cabinet's aggressive policy of invading Manchuria and Mongolia into a small booklet, which has recently been published. After reading this booklet, I was deeply alarmed and felt that every sentence and every word in this booklet had substance, and every sentence and every word could destroy China. Over the past ten days, the Japanese army has forcibly occupied important places in our Liaoning and Jilin provinces, advocated the independence of Manchuria and Mongolia, and done many lawless things, completely inheriting the mantle of the Tanaka Cabinet and implementing the plans in this booklet one by one. At this critical time when the country is in trouble and needs to know itself and its enemy, such a book must be introduced. Please see what he |Tanaka Giichi| said at the beginning of this memorial:

"My empire, in order to develop its resources and cultivate lasting prosperity, has specially established the South Manchuria Railway Company, investing over 444 million yuan in railways, mines, forests, steel, agriculture, animal husbandry, etc. in the area under the beautiful name of Sino-Japanese coexistence and co-prosperity. It is the most ambitious organization in our country's enterprises, and although it is nominally half-official and half-private, the government controls all the real power. The South Manchuria Railway Company is entrusted with diplomatic, police, and general political powers, so that it can exert imperialism and form a special company, no different from the second Korean Governor-General."

Oh, look at his ambition. He has long regarded Manchuria and Mongolia as the second Korea. He wants to seize Manchuria and Mongolia into his own hands forever, so he adopts the following measures: "Moreover, the three eastern provinces are a place of incomplete politics in East Asia. Our Japanese, in order to protect ourselves and protect others, must use iron and blood to remove the difficulties in East Asia. However, if we want to protect the three eastern provinces with the doctrine of iron and blood, the third country, America, will be incited by China to use barbarians to control barbarians to restrain us. At that time, our competition with the United States will be inevitable." "In the future, if we want to control China, we must first overthrow the power of the United States. The meaning is very similar to the Russo-Japanese War."

Now Japan is waging war without declaring it, forcibly occupying important places in the Northeast. Isn't this implementing his doctrine of iron and blood? That's why he uses such a swift and violent means to forcibly occupy, isn't that because he wants to prevent the third country |America| from sanctioning them? On the 29th of last month, Washington sent a telegram stating that |American newspapers have changed their tone due to the Japanese's best efforts to publicize it, and do not support the United States and the League of Nations adopting an intervention policy|, doesn't that mean that they already have a plan to deal with America? At this time, isn't he celebrating the success of his prediction that "If you want to conquer China, you must first conquer Manchuria and Mongolia. If you want to conquer the world, you must first conquer China"? He said in the second section, "Manchuria and Mongolia are not Chinese territory":

"The so-called Manchuria and Mongolia, according to history, are not Chinese territory, nor are they special regions of China. Our Dr. Yano has worked hard to study Chinese history, and all believe that Manchuria and Mongolia are not Chinese territory. This matter has been announced to the world by the Imperial University. Because the research and publication of our Dr. Yano is correct, Chinese scholars have not opposed the theory of our Imperial University."

The reporter is ignorant and has not had the fortune to read Dr. Yano's theory. According to him, our Chinese scholars have not opposed this theory. If this is true, then our scholars who study history and geography cannot shirk their responsibility, and the Institute of History and Philology, which the country has spent a lot of money to establish, does not know what it is doing. Now Japan is vigorously promoting the independence of Manchuria and Mongolia based on these reasons. Tanaka Giichi's disciples and grandsons are truly surpassing their predecessors.

In the section "Korean Immigration Incentives and Protection Policies," there is such a statement: "According to the Koreans in Manchuria and Mongolia, if the number expands to more than 2.5 million, then in times of trouble, Korean people can be used as the basis for military operations, and their actions can be aided in the name of suppression. In addition, among the Koreans in Manchuria and Mongolia, some have naturalized as Chinese citizens, while others have not. At the time of the event, it is a strategy of 'hanging a sheep's head and selling dog meat' to deal with the Korean citizens with Chinese citizenship." After reading this, the Wanbaoshan Incident can be clearly understood, and its conspiracy and trickery are enough to make people gnash their teeth with hatred. There is also a more conspiratorial scheme that will make you shocked:

"We must do our best to prevent the entry and exit of Red Russia. We must use the Fengtian government as a wedge to prevent its power from going south. Our first step is to use the theme of preventing Red Russia from going south to forcibly advance the territory of northern Manchuria by getting an inch and then wanting a foot to seize its resources. In the south, we can control the northward power of China, and in the north, we can control the southward power of Red Russia. If we want to compete with Red Russia politically or economically, we must drive China as a pioneer. We can only supervise China from behind to prevent the expansion of Red Russia, while we secretly cooperate with Red Russia to control the growth of China's power and prevent it from interfering with our vested interests in the South Manchuria Railway."

Oh, it turns out that during the previous Middle East War, Japan strictly maintained neutrality for this reason. Our country must be vigilant in the future to prevent him from succeeding in this way. Regarding the plan of "New Continent Development and the Manchuria-Mongolia Railway," he said this: "The Chinese nation has a large number of troops defending its country, which is economically disadvantageous to us. If we want to develop its resources and expand our national defense, we must vigorously build the North Manchuria Railway. With the opening of this railway, a large number of people can be moved to North Manchuria to control the politics and economy of South Manchuria and to strengthen our national defense to lay the foundation for the overall situation in East Asia. In addition, the completed lines of the South Manchuria Railway are mostly for economic purposes, resulting in a lack of loop lines, which is very unfavorable for wartime mobilization and military supply. In the future, military purposes must be the priority to build a large loop line in Manchuria and Mongolia, which can surround the center of Manchuria and Mongolia to control the military, political, and economic development of China and also prevent the intrusion of Russian forces. This is a necessary key to the creation of our country's new continent." Therefore, he wants to complete the following railways: (1) the Tongliao-Jehol Railway, (2) the Taonan-Solun Railway, (3) a section of the Changtao Railway, (4) the Jihui Railway, (5) the Hunchun-Hailin Railway. Now that they are forcibly occupying our territory, they can do whatever they want, but during the negotiations, they must at least demand the commercial rental rights of these railways. We must remember that these routes are "used for wartime mobilization and military supply," and are sufficient to "control China's military, political, and economic development." We must use strong diplomatic means and vow not to give them to them.

In addition, there are active conspiracies concerning (1) Manchuria-Mongolia trade doctrine, (2) building a large shipping company centered in Dalian to control East Asian maritime transportation, responding to both water and land routes, and dominating the Pacific Ocean, (3) implementing the gold standard in Manchuria, (4) welcoming third-country investment in Manchuria and Mongolia, and (5) changing the management of the South Manchuria Railway Company, as well as the seizure of steel, iron, kerosene, ammonium sulfate, and agricultural fertilizers.
